 Mangalesh Dabral, a man of versatility, was born on 16 May 1948 in Kafalpani, village of Tehri district in Uttarakhand
 vah ek achche lekhak, sampadak va kavi rahe hai
 His famous published works include collection of poems - 'lantern on the mountain', 'way of home', 'what we see', 'the voice is also a place', 'enemy in new age'; The prose collection includes 'once Iowa', 'writer's Bread', 'poet's Loneliness' and a compilation of interviews
 dabraal ne vishwa kaviyon bertolt bresht, haans maounus antsensburger, yanis ritsos, jibagniev herbet, tadeush rukkevich, pablo neruda, ernesto kardenaal, doraa gabe aadi kii kavitaaon kaa angrezi se anuwaad to kiya hi bangla kavi nabarun bhattacharya ke sangrah ‘yah mrityu upatyaka nahin he meraa desh’ ke sah-anuvadak bhi rahe
 Apart from this, Dabral has also done screenwriting for documentaries on litterateurs like Nagarjuna, Nirmal Verma, Mahasweta Devi, UR Ananthamurthy, Gurdial Singh, kurratul-ain Haider
 samaaj, sangeet, cinema or kala par samikshatmak lekhan kiya or bhartiya bhashaaon ke alaava unki kavitaaon ke anuwaad angrezi, roosi, german, dach, francisi, spani, italvi, portugali, balgari, polski aadi videshi bhashaaon ke kai sankalnon or patr-patrikaon main prakashit hote rahe hai
 The Italian translation of his collection of poetry 'awaaz Bhi Ek Place Hai' by Mariola Opredi was published under the name 'anke la voche ai un luogo' and a selection of English translations as 'this number is not an exhaustist'
 vah om prakaash smriti sammaan, shamsher sammaan, pahal sammaan, sahitya academy puraskaar, hindi academy dilli kaa sahityakar sammaan or kumaar vikal smriti sammaan se sammanit hai
 He did poetry recitations during the International Writing Program of the University of Iowa, the Leipzig Book Fair in Germany, the International Poetry Festival of Rotterdam and visits to Nepal, Mauritius and Moscow
 radhakrishna prakaashan se prakashit unke sankalan 'ghar kaa rasta' kii bhoomika likhte hue prayag shukla ne likhaa tha, "mangalesh dabraal kii kavita main roj-marraa jindagi ke sangharsh kii anek anugoonjen or ghar-gaanv or purakhon kii anek aisi smritiyaan hai jo vichlit karti hai
 The sadness of his poetry stems from the atmosphere of our time's tenacity and the deep indifference to human sensations
 yah dukh moolyawaan he kyonki isamen bahut kuch bachaane kii cheshtaa he

 What has been the history of Parbhani seat
 
 
 parabhani loksabhaa seat ke antargat gangakhed, pathari, jintur or parabhani vidhansabha ke alaava jaalnaa jile kii paratur, ghansaavangi vidhansabha seat bhi aati he
 In 1952, Narayan Rao Waghmare won the Lok Sabha elections from the Peasant and Worker's Party of India and reached the Lok Sabha
 unke baad nagarav pangarkar or ramrao narayan yadav 1957 main jite
 Ramrao Narayan Yadav again won in 1962
 phir 1967 or 1971 main shivaji raav deshmukh lagaataar jite, 1977 main sheshrav deshmukh dobaaraa pegent and varkar party of india ko jitaane main safal rahe
 Ramrao Narayanrao Yadav won in 1980 and 1984
 jab shivasena pehali baar jiti or jitate chali gai
 
 
 Shiv Sena first came to this seat in 1989 by winning it
 ashok raav deshmukh saansad chune gaye
 He won again in 1991
 unke baad 1996 main suresh jadhav jite

 ' The Constitution (122nd Amendment) Bill-2014, with a provision to implement the Goods and Services Tax (GST) system, was passed in the Lok Sabha on Wednesday
 vidheyak ke paksh main 336 or vipaksh main 11 mat pade
 10 members were absent during voting on GST Bill
 loksabhaa adhyaksh sumitra mahajan ne kaha ki vidheyak jarurat ke mutabik do-tihaai bahumat se paarit hua he
 Earlier, in response to the discussion on the bill, Union Finance Minister Arun Jaitley denied the opposition's charge that the government is amending certain provisions in the bill without taking the House into confidence
 unhone ise sansadeey samiti ke hawaale kiye jane se bhi inkaar kiya
 He said that the amendments which have been included in the bill, those amendments have already been recommended by the committee on the original bill, so the opposition cannot justify the government on this issue
 arun jetali ne udhaaharan dete hue kaha ki aisa hi ek sanshodhan he GST parishad kii sthapana, jisamen centre or rajya sarkaron ke pratinidhi honge or jo vivaadon kaa nipataara karegi, na ki use supreme court ke sevanivrutt nyaayadhishon kii samiti ke paas bheja jayega
 Jaitley said that a comprehensive consensus has been reached on the bill through a process of extensive deliberations and that the objective of implementing it from April 1, 2016, would not be achieved once it is handed over to the committee
 samvidhan sanshodhan vidheyak ko prabhavi hone ke liye sansad ke donon sadanon se do-tihaai bahumat se paarit hona he or desh ke kul rajyon ke aadhe kii vidhansabhaon dwaara bhi ise paarit hona he
 With the enactment of this bill, most of the indirect taxes of the Center and States will cease to exist, including excise, service tax, value-added tax, sales tax, octroi
 iske lagu hone se kaarobaari desh main kahin bhi apni kaarobaari gatividhiyon kaa vistaar kar sakenge
 Jaitley said, "after the bill comes into effect, the tradition of imposing one tax on another will end
